add_namespace = uk

###########################
# - Opening Lore Event
###########################

country_event = {
	id = uk.1
	title = "State of the Empire"
	desc = uk.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_british_inspect_troops
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = { 
		set_country_flag = has_ministers
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Interesting times ahead"
		news_event = { id = uknews.5 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = uk.80 months = 3 }
			IF = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = uk.10000 hours = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					BHU = { is_ai = yes }
				}
				BHU = { country_event = { id = uk.50000 days = 1 } }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - Empire Day
			ENG = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			CAN = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			NZL = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			AST = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
			SAF = { country_event = { id = ukflavour.50 months = 4 } }
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - Empire Games '38
			country_event = { id = ukflavour.20 months = 26 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {	# - London Economic Conference
			country_event = { id = uk.120 months = 24 }
		}
	}
}

###########################
# - Black Wednesday

add_namespace = ukbw

country_event = {
	id = uk.2
	title = "London Stock Market Crash"
	desc = uk.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		date > 1936.9.1
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			has_war_with = GER
			has_war_with = ITA
			has_war_with = JAP
			has_war_with = USA
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "My God!"
		add_political_power = -50
		add_ideas = ENG_bw
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = ENG
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_stock_crash
			#complete_national_focus = ENG_black_wed 	##### THIS CRASHES THE GAME UNLESS PLAYER CURRENTLY RESEARCHING ANOTHER FOCUS
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = bw_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = bw_tt2
		hidden_effect = {
			FRA = { news_event = { id = worldnews.2 } }
			RAJ = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			NFL = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			AST = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			NZL = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
			SAF = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IMP_bw
					days = 365
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukbw.1
	title = "Factory Closure"
	desc = ukbw.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		OR = {
			has_idea = ENG_bw
			has_idea = ENG_bwa1
			has_idea = ENG_bwa2
			has_idea = ENG_bwa3
			has_idea = ENG_bwa4
			has_idea = ENG_bws1
			has_idea = ENG_bws2
			has_idea = ENG_bws3
			has_idea = ENG_bws4
			has_idea = ENG_bws5
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 12 }
	
	option = {
		name = "Blast!"
		random_list = {
			25 = { 338 = { remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } } }
			25 = { 128 = { remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } } }
			15 = { 123 = { remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } } }
			15 = { 129 = { remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } } }
			15 = { 125 = { remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } } }
			5 = { 121 = { remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 } } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukbw.6
	title = "Successful Policies"
	desc = ukbw.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_conference

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		OR = {
			has_idea = ENG_bw
			has_idea = ENG_bwa1
			has_idea = ENG_bwa2
			has_idea = ENG_bwa3
			has_idea = ENG_bwa4
			has_idea = ENG_bws1
			has_idea = ENG_bws2
			has_idea = ENG_bws3
			has_idea = ENG_bws4
			has_idea = ENG_bws5
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 24 }
	
	option = {
		name = "A good sign"
		add_political_power = 50
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_conservative
				social_conservative < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_liberal
				social_liberal < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				social_democrat < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				paternal_autocrat < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				authoritarian_democrat < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = libertarian_socialist
				libertarian_socialist < 50
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = libertarian_socialist popularity = 0.05 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = uk.3
	title = "A Peaceful Ending at Midnight"
	desc = uk.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		date > 1936.1.20
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "More than a King, a father of a great family."
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = kgv_dead
			retire_country_leader = yes
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = valkist_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = social_conservative_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = social_liberal_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = market_liberal_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "King Edward VIII" 
				desc = "POLITICS_EDWARD_VIII_DESC" 
				picture = "Portrait_Britain_Edward_VIII.dds" 
				expire = "1965.1.1" 
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				traits = { meddler charismatic } 
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes 
						has_country_flag = avenging1776
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = uk.5 months = 5 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes 
						has_country_flag = crushcommunism
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = uk.4 months = 5 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = no
				}
				country_event = { id = uk.400 days = 135 }
			}
		}
	}
}

###########################
# - Assassination/Survival of Edward VIII 
###########################

country_event = {
	id = uk.400
	title = "The King's Commands"
	desc = uk.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_gathering_protest
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "The King commands and we obey"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = 50
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = uk.4 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Maintain the number of bodyguards nearby, whether he likes it or not"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = -50
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			country_event = { id = uk.5 days = 15 }
		}
	}
}

			has_idea = ENG_irb2
			has_idea = ENG_irb3
			has_idea = ENG_irb1
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_crush_brotherhood }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_ire_united }
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_ire_divided }
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ire_rising }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }
	
	option = {
		name = "We must retain control of Ireland!"
		add_political_power = -100
		IRE = { 
			transfer_state = 135
			transfer_state = 134
			transfer_state = 815
			transfer_state = 816
			load_oob = IRE_rising1
			set_capital = 135
			set_stability = 0.5
			set_cosmetic_tag = IRE_FREE
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = IRE
			type = annex_everything
		}
		set_country_flag = ire_gw_rising
		news_event = { id = uknews.6 }
		hidden_effect = {
			add_state_claim = 135
			add_state_claim = 134
			add_state_claim = 815
			load_OOB = ENG_rising_ulster
		}
	}
}

		}

    }
	
	option = {

		}

			has_country_flag = ENG_c_imperial
		}

			target = ARB
			type = annex_everything
		}
    }

			has_country_flag = ENG_c_imperial
		}
        name = "Forget diplomacy, crush them!"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ARB
			type = annex_everything
		}
    }
}

# - Channel Execises (ukf.70-ukf.81)

country_event = {
	id = ukf.70
	title = "Channel Exercises"
	desc = ukf.70.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		is_puppet = no
		has_war = no
		has_navy_size = { size > 100 }
		date > 1939.1.1

# - Removing the Final Roadblock

		}

	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Demand the Kra Isthmus to link our Burma and Malaya colonies"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
		}
		SIA = { country_event = { id = ukf.354 days = 1 } }
	}

		name = "Solve this with war"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = SIA
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.352
	title = "Siam Agrees"
	desc = "The Siamese Government have agreed to our demand to become a protectorate. A wise on their part no doubt."
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Excellent"
		puppet = SIA
		add_to_faction = SIA
		hidden_effect = {
			SIA = { 
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat elections_allowed = no }
				set_political_party = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.2 }
				set_cosmetic_tag = ENG_SIA 
			}
		}
	}
}

# - Strategy in China

country_event = {
	id = ukf.370
	title = "Strategy in China"
	desc = ukf.370.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Fortify Hong Kong from mainland threats(PLACEHOLDER)"
		326 = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = bunker
				level = 3
				province = 10062
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = coastal_bunker
				level = 3
				province = 10062
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = anti_air_building
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = "The Taiwan Purchase"
	desc = ukf.401.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				add = -40
			}
		}
		ENG = { country_event = { id = ukf.402 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We have no use for that island anyway"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				add = 40
			}
		}
		ENG = { country_event = { id = ukf.403 days = 1 } }
	}
}

			target = JAP

			JAP = { is_in_faction_with = ENG }
		}
		name = "Very well"
	}
}

# - London Naval Treaty stuff

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2000
	title = "London Naval Conference"
	desc = ukf.2000.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Let us formalise this treaty with our close friends"
		GRE = { country_event = { id = ukf.2001 days = 1 } }
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { POR = { has_war_with = PRR } }
			}
			POR = { country_event = { id = ukf.2002 days = 1 } }
		}
		set_country_flag = naval_conf
		set_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2001
	title = "London Naval Conference"
	desc = ukf.2001.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Sign the agreement!"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				add = 50
			}
		}
		add_ideas = ALL_lnt
		ENG = { give_guarantee = GRE }
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = { modify_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value = 1 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We won't sign this ridiculous bit of paper"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				add = -50
			}
		}
		ENG = { country_event = { id = ukf.2003 } }
	}
}

# - Jutland/Dover Pact

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2100
	title = "The Jutland Pact"
	desc = ukf.2100.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "We must avoid another naval race with Germany"
		GER = { country_event = { id = ukf.2101 days = 1 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2101
	title = "The Jutland Pact"
	desc = ukf.2101.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "This will ensure peace between our two nations"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				add = 30
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = ITA
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = SOV
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 74 }
				add = 25
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = ENG_jpact
			target = ENG
		}
		add_ideas = ENG_jutpact
		ENG = { give_guarantee = GER }
		ENG = { country_event = { id = ukf.2102 days = 1 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG = { modify_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value = 2 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Limit our naval development? I think not!"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				add = -30
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = ITA
				add = -20
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war_with = SOV
				add = -50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 74 }
				add = -25
			}
		}
		ENG = { country_event = { id = ukf.2103 days = 1 } }
	}
}

	id = ukf.2102
	title = "Germany signs the pact"

	is_triggered_only = yes

		}
		set_country_flag = jutlandaccord
	}
}

# - London Naval Treaty membership checker

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2500
	title = "London Naval Treaty Membership"
	desc = ukf.2500.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_country_flag = naval_conf
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value > 1 }
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value < 4 }
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt1 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1 
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The London Naval Treaty ensures naval security"
		add_ideas = ENG_lnt1
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = ENG
			}
			add_ideas = IMP_lnt
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2501
	title = "London Naval Treaty Membership"
	desc = ukf.2500.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_country_flag = naval_conf
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value > 3 }
			has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value < 6 }
		}
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt2 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1 
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The London Naval Treaty ensures naval security"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = ENG_lnt1 add_idea = ENG_lnt2 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukf.2502
	title = "London Naval Treaty Membership"
	desc = ukf.2500.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	fire_only_once = no
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ENG
		has_country_flag = naval_conf
		has_country_flag = { flag = lnt_members value > 5 }
		NOT = { has_idea = ENG_lnt3 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1 
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The London Naval Treaty ensures naval security"
		swap_ideas = { remove_idea = ENG_lnt2 add_idea = ENG_lnt3 }

country_event = {		# - France
	id = ukf.5000
	title = "The Second Great War"
	desc = ukf.5000.d
	picture = report_event_merchant_ship_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

    fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "We cannot allow France to fall to the Germans, we must involve ourselves directly"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = reformentente
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				add = -100
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			GER = { NOT = { has_idea = ENG_jutpact } }
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = GER
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = isolation
			}
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = isolation add_idea = civilian_economy }
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		set_country_flag = decided_gw2
		set_country_flag = gw2intervention
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Send the French equipment and ''volunteers''"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = reformentente
				add = -50
			}
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = -10000 producer = ENG }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = -500 producer = ENG }
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = -500 producer = ENG }
		add_manpower = -50000
		FRA = { country_event = { id = ukf.5001 } }
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = isolation
			}
			swap_ideas = { remove_idea = isolation add_idea = civilian_economy }
		}
		set_country_flag = decided_gw2
		set_country_flag = gw2intervention
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					GER = { NOT = { has_idea = ENG_jutpact } }
				}
				country_event = { id = ukf.5002 days = 30 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "We have no interest in this right now"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = avenging1776
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = challengefrance
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = isoimpfed
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = capesingapore
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				has_war = yes
				add = 100
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = deciding_gw2
	}
}

    }

				NOT = { original_tag = SAF }

    desc = uknews.9.d

    major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		IF = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						original_tag = FRA
						original_tag = ITA
						original_tag = USA
						original_tag = JAP
					}
					OR = {
						has_government = valkist 
						has_government = paternal_autocrat 
						has_government = libertarian_socialist 
						has_government = collectivist 
						has_government = vanguardist 
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = lec1
		}
	}

    option =  {
        trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = ENG
				AND = {
					original_tag = FRA
					NOT = { has_government = valkist }
					NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
					NOT = { has_government = libertarian_socialist }
					NOT = { has_government = collectivist }
					NOT = { has_government = vanguardist }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = USA
					NOT = { has_government = valkist }
					NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
					NOT = { has_government = libertarian_socialist }
					NOT = { has_government = collectivist }
					NOT = { has_government = vanguardist }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = ITA
					NOT = { has_government = valkist }
					NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
					NOT = { has_government = libertarian_socialist }
					NOT = { has_government = collectivist }
					NOT = { has_government = vanguardist }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
				}
				AND = {
					original_tag = JAP
					NOT = { has_government = valkist }
					NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
					NOT = { has_government = libertarian_socialist }
					NOT = { has_government = collectivist }
					NOT = { has_government = vanguardist }
					NOT = { has_war_with = ENG }
				}
			}
        }
        name = "Only through co-operation can economic difficulties be lessened"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = eco_conf1
			days = 365
		}
    }

				AND = {
					NOT = { original_tag = ENG }

	desc = emp.1.d

		IF = {
			limit = {
				ENG = { has_country_flag = indust37 }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IMP_workshop
				days = 180
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				ENG = { has_country_flag = infra37 }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IMP_infrastructure
				days = 180
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				ENG = { has_country_flag = milbase37 }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = IMP_milbase
				days = 180
			}
		}
	}
}

# - Future of the Empire
# - Status Quo

country_event = {
	id = emp.2
	title = "Britain pursues Imperial Status Quo"
	desc = emp.2.d
	picture = report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			tag = CAN
		}
		name = "This is unacceptable!"
		ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.3 days = 1 } }
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				original_tag = RAJ
				ENG = { has_country_flag = india_truce }
			}
		}
		name = "This will surely only add fuel to the rebellion."
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						ENG = { has_country_flag = india_truce }
						ENG = { NOT = { has_country_flag = capesingapore } }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = emp.8 months = 1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = emp.8 months = 1 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = CAN 
					AND = {
						original_tag = RAJ
						ENG = { has_country_flag = india_truce }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = "The Status Quo ensures stability at least."
	}
}

					has_opinion = { target = ENG value < 0 }
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = NZL
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				}
				add = -25
			}
			#-RAJ MODIFIER
			modifier = {
				original_tag = RAJ
				add = 50
			}
			#-SAF MODIFIERS
			modifier = {
				original_tag = SAF
				add = 45
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = SAF
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value < 0 }
				}
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					original_tag = SAF
					has_opinion = { target = ENG value > 49 }
				}
				add = -25
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = rejects_federation
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = CAN
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.16 days = 1 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = AST
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.17 days = 4 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SAF
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.18 days = 2 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = RAJ
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.19 days = 3 } }
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = NZL
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = emp.20 days = 5 } }
		}
	}
}

			controls_state = 440
			controls_state = 883
			controls_state = 441
			controls_state = 445
			controls_state = 442
			controls_state = 811
		}
		has_war = no 
		is_ai = no
		has_country_flag = reconquering_india
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }
	
	option = {
		name = "The Raj shall be restored to its former glory"
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_core_of = RAJ
			}
			RAJ = { transfer_state = PREV }
			IF = {		# Hopefully this will stop Raj becoming stupidly OP
				limit = {
					industrial_complex > 3
					industrial_complex < 8
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 3 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					industrial_complex > 8		# why
				}
				remove_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 5 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					arms_factory > 3
					arms_factory < 8
				}
				remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 3 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					arms_factory > 8		# why
				}
				remove_building = { type = arms_factory level = 5 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					dockyard > 3
					dockyard < 8
				}
				remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 3 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					dockyard > 8		# why
				}
				remove_building = { type = dockyard level = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = emp.51
	title = "Canada Responds"
	desc = {
		trigger = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } }
		text = emp.51a.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { NOT = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } } }
		text = emp.51b.d
	}
	picture = report_event_generic_conference
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		trigger = { 
			CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } 
		}
		name = "Excellent"
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } }
		}
		name = "Let them go!"
		end_puppet = CAN
		remove_from_faction = CAN
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { CAN = { has_country_flag = accepts_federation } }
		}
		name = "We will restore order to our territory!"
		end_puppet = CAN
		remove_from_faction = CAN
		declare_war_on = {
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = CAN
		}
	}
}

		name = "Send them equipment and volunteers!"

			base = 50

				has_war_with = ENG

			}
			modifier = {
				original_tag = HOL
				add = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				original_tag = FRA
				add = 30
			}
			modifier = {
				original_tag = GER
				add = 25
			}

			limit = {
				original_tag = FRA
			}

			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment amount = -100 producer = FRA }

	id = uknews.100
	title = "The Fall of Paris"
	desc = uknews.100.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_german_soldiers
	
	major = yes
	
	trigger = {
		16 = { is_controlled_by = ENG }
		16 = { is_owned_by = FRA }
		FRA = { has_war_with = ENG }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = fop_eng }
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = fop_eng
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "France's future is now in question"
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				TAG = ENG
				TAG = FRA
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "Splendid work gentlemen"
		trigger = { TAG = ENG }
	}
	option = {
		name = "We will reclaim Paris from those damn Brits!"
		trigger = { TAG = FRA }
	}
}

add_namespace = eng

# Hungary asks to join Imperial Protection Alliance
country_event = {
		id = eng.2000
		title = eng.2000.t
		desc = eng.2000.d
		picture = GFX_news_event_aid_pact

		is_triggered_only = yes

		fire_only_once = yes

		option = { # accept
			name = eng.2001a
			ai_chance = {
				base = 100
				modifier = {
					add = -25
					HUN = { has_army_size = { size < 5 } }
				}
				modifier = {
					add = 100
					HUN = { has_army_size = { size > 10 } }
				}
			}
			ENG = { add_to_faction = HUN }
			HUN = {
				country_event = { hours = 2 id = hungary.2250}
			}
		}

		option = { # decline
			name = eng.2002.a
			ai_chance = {
				base = 0
				modifier = {
					add = +25
					HUN = { has_army_size = { size < 5 } }
				}
			}
			HUN = {
				country_event = { hours = 2 id = hungary.2750 }
			}
		}
}


# Italy wants to buy Malta - added by Drowse

	id = uk.3000
	title = uk.3000.t
	desc = uk.3000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_malta

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Sell Malta
		name = uk.3000.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_political_power = -75
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ENG_malta_sold
			days = 365
		}
		ITA = {
			transfer_state = 116
			country_event = { id = italy.65 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Keep Malta
		name = uk.3000.b
		ai_chance = { base = 90 }
		add_political_power = 25
		ITA = {
			country_event = { id = italy.66 }
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = ukfate.4
	title = "The Fate of the United States"
	desc = ukfate.4.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = "Give New England to Canada, annex the Eastern sea-board and establish a puppet Government."
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				region = 197
			}
			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		release_puppet = USA
		USA = { set_cosmetic_tag = ENG_USA }
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					region = 117
				}
				ENG = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { MEX = { controls_state = 743 } }
				}
				USA = { transfer_state = 743 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { MEX = { controls_state = 484 } }
				}
				USA = { transfer_state = 484 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Create a Dominion of North America"
		release_puppet = USA
		USA = { set_cosmetic_tag = ENG_USA }
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { MEX = { controls_state = 743 } }
				}
				USA = { transfer_state = 743 }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { MEX = { controls_state = 484 } }
				}
				USA = { transfer_state = 484 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Maintain occupation"
	}
}
